<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перепутаться.html>перепу́таться</a> (27287)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепутать.html>перепу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perepútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепутаться.html>перепу́таться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepútatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перепу́тываться</b>)

***перерабатывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перерабатывать.html>перераба́тывать</a> (29052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработать.html>перерабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pererabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерабатывать.html>перераба́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererabátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработать.html>перерабо́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to process <i>(into)</i>, to work <i>(into)</i>, to convert <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to remake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерабатывать.html>перераба́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>статью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererabátyvatʹ</b> statʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to recast/edit an article</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exceed the fixed hours of work, to work overtime</li>
<li>to overwork</li></ol>

***переработать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переработать.html>перерабо́тать</a> (22663)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработать.html>перерабо́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererabótatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерабатывать.html>перераба́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to process <i>(into)</i>, to work <i>(into)</i>, to convert <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to remake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переработать.html>перерабо́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>статью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererabótatʹ</b> statʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to recast/edit an article</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработанный.html>перерабо́танное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:издание.html>изда́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pererabótannoje izdánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">revised edition</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exceed the fixed hours of work, to work overtime</li>
<li>to overwork</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererabótka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>processing, treatment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрасль.html>о́трасль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́тке</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сельскохозяйственный.html>сельскохозя́йственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырье.html>сырья́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ótraslʹ po <b>pererabótke</b> selʹskoxozjájstvennovo syrʹjá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">produce processing industry</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отход.html>отхо́дов</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererabótka</b> otxódov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">recycling</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>remaking, revision, revised version
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуться.html>подве́рглась</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переработка.html>перерабо́тке</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kníga podvérglasʹ <b>pererabótke</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the book was revised</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***перерастать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перерастать.html>перераста́ть</a> (19202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерасти.html>перерасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pererastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерастать.html>перераста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererastátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерасти.html>перерасти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to <i>(over)</i>top, to outgrow, to outstrip</li>
<li>to develop <i>(into)</i>, to grow <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to be too old <i>(for)</i>, to be past the stage <i>(for)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***перерасти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перерасти.html>перерасти́</a> (18270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерасти.html>перерасти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерастать.html>перераста́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to <i>(over)</i>top, to outgrow, to outstrip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерасти.html>переро́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отца́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on užé <b>pererós</b> otcá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is already taller than his father</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to develop <i>(into)</i>, to grow <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to be too old <i>(for)</i>, to be past the stage <i>(for)</i></li></ol>

***перерезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перереза́ть</a> (8215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererézatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перереза́ть</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перере́зывать</b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><i>(all or many)</i> to kill, to slaughter</li>
<li>to cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веревка.html>верёвку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererézatʹ</b> verjóvku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut the rope</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererézatʹ</b> komú-libo dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to block someone's path</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́телю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отступление.html>отступле́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererézatʹ</b> neprijátelju putʹ k otstupléniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off the enemy's line of retreat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut <i>(across)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pererézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перереза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перереза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веревка.html>верёвку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererezátʹ</b> verjóvku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut the rope</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перереза́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererezátʹ</b> komú-libo dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to block someone's path</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перереза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́телю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отступление.html>отступле́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pererezátʹ</b> neprijátelju putʹ k otstupléniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off the enemy's line of retreat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut <i>(across)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перерыв.html>переры́в</a> (3573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прерывать.html>прерыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерыв.html>переры́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pererýv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерыв.html>переры́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерыв.html>переры́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перерыв.html>переры́вов</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>рыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пересадить.html>пересади́ть</a> (22123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересадить.html>пересади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peresadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересаживать.html>переса́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make a (small) change in one's seat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподаватель.html>преподава́тель</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пересадить.html>пересади́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ученик.html>ученико́в</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prepodavátelʹ <b>peresadíl</b> učenikóv</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the teacher made the pupils change their seats [moved his pupils round]</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to transplant, to graft</li></ol>
